- Sporadic, awkward "Spider-Man explained" segments that overcorrect into hagiography — he praises the wrong feats, misses what is actually impressive, and audibly overpronounces Parker's name when referring to him in third person, which a voice-pattern analyst would flag as compensatory overarticulation.
- Confessional segments, brief, usually late in episodes when fatigue lowers the defensive baseline. He has said on record, more than once, that "I got some things wrong." He has never said what.

---

## 3. The Kindred / Sins Rising / Last Remains Period

During the Spencer run's escalation toward *Last Remains* and the Kindred arc (2020–2021), the subject is operationally peripheral but emotionally instrumented. Two data points warrant inclusion:

- He is among the small circle Parker confides in unevenly during the Kindred crisis, and the subject's response — *to call*, repeatedly, when Parker goes dark — is one of the cleanest pieces of evidence in the file that the post-unmasking reorientation is real and not performative. The subject does not call people he does not care about. He sends bills.
- The arc's surfacing of Harry Osborn material, and the broader recurrence of sins-of-the-father motifs throughout the period, runs in close thematic parallel to the subject's own unresolved paternal material (J. Jonah Sr.'s exposure as conman and bigamist, see §2/§3 of the working file). The subject is not depicted as consciously connecting these — but his behavior during the period is markedly more brittle than the prior eighteen months, and a surveillance-grade reading would not treat that as coincidence.

---

## 4. The Beyond Corporation Interregnum

During the *Beyond* arc (Wells/Zeb/Ahmed/Gleason et al., ASM vol. 6, ~2021–2022), with Ben Reilly briefly operating as the sanctioned, corporate-licensed Spider-Man and Parker hospitalized, the subject's positioning is diagnostically rich.

He neither fully endorses nor fully rejects the corporate Spider-Man. The publicly stated position is something like cautious approval of the accountability structure (a Spider-Man with an employer is, in his ideology, categorically less threatening than a Spider-Man with a mask and no payroll). The privately observable position is markedly less enthusiastic — his podcast tone when discussing the corporate operation is flatter, more procedural, less invested than when discussing Parker. **Intelligence read: he prefers the Spider-Man he hated for thirty years to the Spider-Man he should ideologically prefer.** This is the most concise possible proof that his Parker-hostility was always reaction formation. Strip the mask off and he is, against his stated worldview, attached.

When the Beyond arrangement collapses and Parker resumes operations, the subject's podcast tempo accelerates measurably within the canonical depiction. He has his interlocutor back.

---

## 5. Gang War, Dark Web Fallout, and Civic Re-engagement

Through the Wells-era *Dark Web* and *Gang War* sequences (2022–2024), the subject's documented appearances cluster around three behaviors:

- **Civic editorializing on organized crime.** This is the oldest and most stable register in his entire file — the Kingpin/Hammerhead/Madame Masque material activates the sublimation channel cleanly, and the subject is at his most coherent and least dysregulated when speaking on it. The voice flattens, the cadence slows, the cigar-jabbing gestures (still observable on video podcasts) become more deliberate.
- **Hostage-adjacent incidents.** The subject's lifetime base-rate for being personally caught up in costumed-crime collateral remains elevated relative to civilian norms. During Gang War he is briefly endangered and reacts, on camera, with the paradoxical clarity the file has documented at high-arousal crisis grade since the Lee era. No cardiac event.
- **Re-engagement with municipal figures.** Quiet records of him taking meetings with current City Hall staff, former mayoral-office aides, and at least one Federal liaison. He is not running for office. He is keeping the relationship infrastructure warm. This is consistent with a man who has held the mayoralty once and tells himself he will never run again while behaving exactly as a man who might.

---

## 6. The John Jameson Variable

The son remains, across the most recent period, the single most reliable destabilizer and re-stabilizer of the subject's affect. Recent canonical material has continued to subject John to enhancement-related episodes (Man-Wolf reversions; cosmic-tech entanglements in various crossover material). Each episode produces the same observable sequence in the subject:

1. Refusal to discuss publicly.
2. Immediate cessation of unrelated grievance content on the podcast feed (the absence is itself the signal — surveillance would track episode-cadence interruptions).
3. Direct, unguarded outreach to Parker and/or other enhanced individuals he has spent decades attacking, asking for help. He does not soften the ask with apology; he simply makes it, and they help him, every time, which is a piece of intelligence about the wider hero community's read of the subject that the file should note.
4. Post-resolution, return to baseline irritability, often elevated for two to three weeks.

The pattern is consistent across every John-crisis since the Conway era and there is no reason to expect it to vary. **The son is the only person on Earth in whose presence the subject does not perform.**

---

## 7. The Father Material — Continued Non-Metabolization

J. Jonah Jameson Sr.'s exposure as a long-term abuser, conman, and bigamist (modern-era retcon, Waid/Slott period) remains, in the most recent record, the subject's least processed material. He does not discuss it on the podcast. He has not written a book about it. He has not, per any available record, sought therapy. The avoidance is total and, given the file's overall pattern of the body absorbing what consciousness refuses, almost certainly load-bearing on the residual cardiovascular risk. A medical actuary reading this file would price his ten-year cardiac event probability significantly above demographic baseline on this datum alone.

The recent canonical surfacing of Sr.-related material (cameo appearances, references in family scenes with John, occasional flashback material) produces in the subject the most reliable affective tell in the late-period file: **he leaves the room.** Not metaphorically. He physically exits whatever space the reference occurred in, often mid-sentence, often returning ten to forty minutes later with no acknowledgment of the absence. Subordinates have learned not to follow.

---

## 8. Social and Domestic Footprint, Present Day

**Residence.** Manhattan, post-mayoral. Apartment, not the brownstone of earlier eras; he has downsized since Marla's death and has not re-expanded. The apartment is, by all available description, under-furnished, over-papered (newsprint, files, podcast notes in physical form — he does not trust cloud storage and prints), and contains exactly one framed photograph of Marla in a place where he sees it from the desk.

**Routine.** Surveillance-grade reconstruction of the current weekly pattern, derived from podcast cadence, public appearances, and canonical depiction:
- Early riser, pre-0600. Coffee — black, volume extreme, the caffeine intake noted in §2 of the working file undiminished.
- Morning: news intake across multiple feeds, print where available; he marks up physical copy with a pen, a habit dating to the Bugle copy-desk years.
- Mid-morning to early afternoon: podcast production, often solo recording, occasional guests. Records standing when he is angry, seated when he is tired; the posture is audible in the audio if one knows to listen for chair noise.
- Late afternoon: meetings, calls, civic correspondence. He still answers his own phone for a short list of numbers (Robbie, John, certain former staff, Parker now intermittently).
- Evening: meal, often solo, often at one of two or three long-standing Manhattan establishments where the staff know him and the seat is held. Tips well. Does not linger.
- Night: more reading, occasional second short recording session for international feeds, sleep late and poorly.

**Relational map, current.**
- **Robbie Robertson** — sustained, the longest unbroken professional/personal relationship in his life, the conscience he externalizes when he cannot locate his own. Contact frequency: at least weekly, often daily during news cycles.
- **John Jameson** — see §6. Asymmetric: the subject calls more than he is called.
- **Peter Parker** — post-unmasking, slowly normalized. Contact awkward but real. The subject has, on at least one occasion in recent canon, used Parker's first name without sarcasm, which is a measurable shift.
- **Betty Brant, Ben Urich, surviving Bugle alumni** — periodic. The bond from the §3 pattern (subordinates who survived the first six months become permanent family) holds.
- **Marla** — daily, internally. The subject talks to her, per canonical depiction; not with delusion, with the ordinary widower's habit. The file should record this as a sign of preserved attachment capacity, not pathology.
- **Romantic** — no current partner of record. The file should not expect one. He is not looking and would not recognize the search if he undertook it.

---

## 9. Public Profile and Reputational Trajectory

The subject's current public profile is a curious composite: half elder-statesman of New York journalism, half clownish reactionary podcaster, half (the math is wrong, which is the point) genuinely reformed witness to a hero he spent decades miscalibrating. Different constituencies hold different versions:

- To older Manhattan readership: a Bugle institution, slightly diminished but respected.
- To the hero community: a known quantity, no longer hostile by default, treated with cautious courtesy by most and with genuine warmth by a small number (Parker, the Fantastic Four in some periods, certain Avengers liaisons).
- To his podcast audience: a brand, with the brand's tolerances for inconsistency.
- To former political opponents: a known opportunist who governed harder than expected and quit when his wife was killed, which earned him a measure of grace he would not otherwise have received.

He is aware of all four reads and manages none of them consciously.

---

## 10. Current Pressure-Point Status

Updating §3's pressure points to present:

- **The Scorpion** — Gargan remains active in canon. Each Gargan appearance reactivates the subject's oldest guilt. No cardiac event since *The Pulse*, but baseline elevation is observable for days after a Gargan headline.
- **The father** — fully unmetabolized, leaves-the-room response, see §7.
- **Marla** — stabilized into the ordinary structure of grief; no longer eruptive, now sedimented. The widower's daily small conversation has taken the place of the rage register.
- **The unmasking** — partially metabolized through the podcasting pivot and direct contact with Parker. Not fully. He still has not said, in any registered medium, that he was wrong in proportion to having been wrong.
- **Cowardice (the Sin-Eater master key)** — the gap remains, and the podcast format both relieves and renews it. He performs courage by talking and still has not, by his own private accounting, risked his body for anyone but his son.

---

## 11. Present Assessment — Where He Is, How He Got Here

The subject is, at present, in the most stable late-life configuration the file has ever recorded — and "stable" is doing specific work: it means the dysregulation is distributed across more, smaller channels (daily podcast venting, civic editorializing, occasional outreach to long-bond contacts) rather than concentrated in the few large channels (Bugle masthead, mayoral office, Spider-Man crusade) that historically produced catastrophic somatic loads. The cardiovascular system has been spared major events for years. The sublimation channel is intact and productive. The attachment to a small circle is preserved. The capacity for update, demonstrated by the post-unmasking reorientation, has been shown to be real, even if costly and incomplete.

He got here by surviving: his father's house, the Scorpion's existence, the Kingpin's lobby, Marla's death, his own coronary, the unmasking, the mayoralty, the loss of the print platform he built his life around. He got here by being, despite his worst instincts, capable of loyalty, work, and grief. He got here by being wrong about one specific man for a very long time and then, in his fashion — slow, partial, ungraceful, real — being less wrong.

The file's working forecast: he will continue podcasting until a cardiac or cerebrovascular event removes the option. He will not retire. He will, with one or two further John-crises or Gargan resurfacings, produce one more late-life destabilization, survive it, and resume. He will not write the memoir that would require him to address his father in full; if he ever does, it will be the final somatic test and the file should be ready for it. He will die at a desk, of his own pattern, and the last thing he says will be either a correction or a complaint, and either way Robbie Robertson will be the one called first.

That is the current state. The next section moves to behavioral micro-pattern and somatic tells, where the day-to-day surveillance grain lives.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — JOHN JONAH JAMESON, JR.

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, hospital records cross-referenced with Bugle insurance filings, Sloan-Kettering and Mount Sinai admissions, NYC mayoral physical disclosures (2008–2011), photographic record, and panel-by-panel somatic observation across the canonical period. Subject DOB inferred from WWII service references; presents in primary record from early forties onward.*

---

## 1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

Subject is a Caucasian male of medium height (estimated 5'9"–5'10"), mesomorphic build trending stocky with age, broad-shouldered, short-necked — a body type with elevated baseline cardiovascular risk independent of behavior. Resting heart rate, where observable through carotid pulsation under stress, is chronically elevated; the neck vessels are prominent enough to be a visible behavioral tell long before they are a clinical finding. Skin tone is florid at baseline, ruddier under affect, mottling toward the cheeks and the bridge of the nose with sustained arousal — a vasomotor pattern consistent with longstanding essential hypertension, alcohol-independent flushing, and possible rosacea (the nasolabial telangiectasia visible in close-quarters reference images is unlikely to be drawn-in; it tracks with the documented cigar and caffeine load).

Sleep architecture: insufficient, fragmented, militantly defended as a virtue. Subject is observed at the Bugle at 0530 multiple times per week across decades and is frequently the last person on the floor at 2300. Naps, never; coffee, perpetually; the body has not had a full restorative sleep cycle on a regular basis since the Eisenhower administration. The chronic sleep deficit potentiates every other condition in this file — hypertension, glucose handling, irritability threshold, ulcer relapse.

Posture: forward-shouldered, neck protracted, jaw thrust slightly forward at rest — a chronic sympathetic-tone postural set, "ready to bark." Cervical and upper-trapezius hypertonicity is implied by the recurring depiction of him rubbing the back of his neck with the heel of his hand during exposition scenes; this is also one of the file's reliable pre-MI prodromes.

---

## 2. CHILDHOOD AND DEVELOPMENTAL TRAUMA — THE FOUNDATIONAL PHYSICAL INSULT

The single most important entry in this section is the one with no contemporaneous medical record: sustained physical abuse from J. Jonah Jameson, Sr. across childhood and early adolescence, disclosed in the modern record (Waid, Slott). The somatic consequences predict the entire adult medical chart.

Repeated blows to the head, torso, and back during a developing nervous system produce: chronic baseline sympathetic activation; impaired vagal tone; lowered threshold for the startle response (subject's documented adult flinch on unexpected window-impact during Spider-Man arrivals is florid and reflexive, not theatrical); and the HPA-axis dysregulation that will manifest in adulthood as the ulcer-hypertension-MI cascade. The body learned, before language, that the environment was a source of unpredictable physical danger from a powerful concealed-intent figure. Every later condition in this file is, in part, that lesson expressed in tissue.

There is no record of any childhood medical intervention for these injuries; the era and the family pattern make it certain that emergency presentations, if any, were attributed to "falls." The lifelong dental record (the teeth are intact, the bite class appears normal in close-mouth panels) suggests the blows were predominantly to the body and the back of the head rather than to the face — consistent with an abuser who knew to hide the work.

---

## 3. MILITARY SERVICE — INTERVENING TRAUMA AND ITS REINFORCEMENT

Subject's WWII service (referenced in multiple writers, made explicit in modern flashback) places him in combat-adjacent or combat theater in his late teens to early twenties. The medical relevance is double: first, a second confirming round of high-intensity stress imprinting on an already-traumatized nervous system; second, the period during which the cigar habit was almost certainly established (military-issue tobacco, the Greatest Generation's universal accelerant). No record of combat wounding survives in canon; no Purple Heart is asserted. The most likely physiological residue is sub-threshold PTSD layered onto the developmental trauma, presenting in adulthood as the affect profile in §3 of the analytical workup — paradoxical calm under acute physical threat, dysregulation under ambiguity.

---

## 4. THE GASTROINTESTINAL FILE — PEPTIC ULCER DISEASE, CHRONIC DYSPEPSIA

The ulcer is the oldest documented adult condition and predates Spider-Man in subject's life. It is mentioned in the Lee/Ditko run within the first dozen issues, treated as established fact: he is on antacids, his physician has warned him, the staff know. This is the single most important diagnostic fact in the file: the dysregulation that the Spider-Man fixation will later be hung upon is already physically inscribed in the gastric mucosa before the fixation has its object.

Best characterization: duodenal ulcer, chronic, recurrent, with episodic gastric involvement; superimposed nonerosive gastritis; functional dyspepsia between active episodes. Likely H. pylori-positive given the era of onset and the absence of any documented eradication regimen until at least the 1990s. The pharmaceutical record across the run shows him moving through the eras of acid suppression as the science moved: aluminum-magnesium chewables and effervescent antacids in the early period (the white chalky residue on the desk, the bicarbonate glass of water as a recurrent prop); H2 blockers in the late 1970s through 1980s (cimetidine, then ranitidine); proton pump inhibitors from the 1990s forward (omeprazole, later esomeprazole). The bottle on the desk changes; the underlying pathology does not.

Symptom pattern: epigastric burning two to three hours postprandial, classically relieved by food and recurrence-defined by stress. Subject is observed eating at the desk, fast, frequently, and badly — pastrami sandwiches, deli soup, anything Betty Brant or a copy boy will bring — which both feeds the ulcer-relief reflex and ensures the cycle continues. The "pickle on the side" and the "no, the pickle is on the wrong side" outburst pattern is, somatically, an irritable man pre-empting reflux.

Psychological impact: the ulcer is the body that he cannot shout down. It is the first thing in his life that does not flinch. He hates it for that and treats it with the displaced contempt he would direct at a recalcitrant junior reporter. He has never once, in the record, named the ulcer as evidence that his way of life is unsustainable; he has named it many times as evidence that his subordinates are killing him.

---

## 5. CARDIOVASCULAR FILE — HYPERTENSION, ATHEROSCLEROTIC DISEASE, MYOCARDIAL INFARCTION

**Essential hypertension**, untreated or undertreated for decades, is implied from the earliest record and confirmed in implication by the 2004–2005 cardiac event. The clinical picture across the run: florid facial flushing on minor provocation; visible carotid and temporal vessel engorgement during outbursts; episodes of post-rage dizziness, ear ringing, and brief disorientation that resolve when he sits down; at least two documented episodes of near-syncope at the Bugle. He has been told by physicians to take antihypertensives; he is intermittently compliant; he resents the medication as a daily reminder that he is not in charge of his body. The likely regimen evolution: thiazide diuretic in the early decades (poorly tolerated due to the urinary frequency he refuses to plan editorial meetings around), beta blocker added in middle period (he hates it — it blunts the affect he uses as a managerial instrument and contributes to the documented mid-period weight gain and the brief period of erectile dysfunction implied around the Marla-marriage adjustment), ACE inhibitor or ARB in the post-MI period as the gold standard.

**Hyperlipidemia**, near-certain by middle age given the diet, the body habitus, the inactivity, and the genetic loading implied by an abusive father whose own cardiovascular history is unknown but likely poor. Statin therapy post-MI is a near-certainty.

**The myocardial event (Bendis, *The Pulse*, 2004–2005).** Inferior or anterolateral MI precipitated by the acute sympathetic surge during the Gargan/Venom confrontation in the Bugle offices. Presentation: crushing substernal pain, diaphoresis, radiation likely to left arm and jaw, denial for some minutes (he tries to keep working — this is documented and is the most Jameson thing in the cardiac record), collapse witnessed by staff. ED course presumably included troponin confirmation, cardiac catheterization, and either percutaneous intervention with stenting (most likely, given the era and his recovery trajectory) or, less likely, single-vessel bypass. Post-MI ejection fraction not formally disclosed but his return to full work capacity within months suggests preserved or mildly reduced systolic function.

Post-MI medical regimen, reconstructed: dual antiplatelet therapy for the standard year (aspirin lifelong, clopidogrel for the index period); high-intensity statin; beta blocker (which he tolerates better now that the alternative is dying); ACE inhibitor; sublingual nitroglycerin in the desk drawer as a prn for angina (the small brown bottle visible in later panels). Cardiac rehabilitation: nominally enrolled, episodically attended, mostly ignored. He walks more after the MI — to the Bugle, around the office, around Gracie Mansion later — but he does not exercise in any structured sense. The walking is a concession, not a program.

**The Marla-death stress cardiomyopathy / probable second event.** During and after the Spider-Island arc and Marla's killing, subject sustains a sustained period of physiological grief that, in a man of his cardiac substrate, almost certainly involved at least one subclinical or clinically minor cardiac event — chest pain presentations, telemetry admissions, ruled-out or ruled-in NSTEMI episodes. The record does not name a second MI explicitly, but the resignation from the mayoralty and the visible aging in the post-Spider-Island appearances are consistent with a second insult to the myocardium and to whatever was left of his denial.

Psychological impact of the cardiac file: the MI is the bill from §2 arriving in §5. Forty years after the Scorpion decision, his own funded creation comes to kill him and the body cooperates. The event reorganizes nothing in his stated worldview but reorganizes a great deal in his behavior — quieter mornings, the toupee adjusted less aggressively, the cigar reduced, a tendency to sit before shouting rather than shouting while standing. He has not made peace with mortality; he has made an uneasy professional arrangement with it.

---

## 6. TRAUMA — KIDNAPPINGS, ASSAULTS, INCIDENT-RELATED INJURIES

Subject has been taken hostage, assaulted, or directly endangered by costumed adversaries at a rate far above civilian baseline. Partial enumeration:

- **Spider-Slayer incidents (multiple, 1960s through 2000s).** Pilot injuries from the original ASM #25 incident (he himself piloted Smythe's first unit — abrasions, soft-tissue, ego). Later abductions by Spencer and Alistair Smythe units include blunt trauma from restraint mechanisms, near-asphyxiation, and at least one incident of restraint-related rhabdomyolysis-grade muscle compression.
- **Scorpion confrontations.** Direct assaults by Mac Gargan across decades; subject has been thrown, struck, and on one occasion (Bendis, *Pulse*) cornered to the point of cardiac event. Tail-strike contusion injuries to the torso documented in at least two arcs.
- **Hobgoblin incident.** Held, threatened, exposed to Hobgoblin's pumpkin-bomb pyrotechnics; presumptive minor blast injury and flash exposure — tinnitus likely sequela.
- **Venom (Brock) confrontations.** Held by symbiote, near-asphyxiated, psychological trauma severe.
- **Sin-Eater era.** Witnessed and proximate to Captain Stacy-adjacent and Jean DeWolff-adjacent violence; not directly assaulted but in scene-of-incident proximity.
- **Mayoral-era assassination attempts and Anti-Spider Squad operational incidents.** Various blunt-force, blast-adjacent, and fall-risk events.
- **Spider-Island / Marla's killing.** Subject was physically present at the killing of his wife by an Alistair Smythe Spider-Slayer descendant. Mechanism of Marla's death: blade/tail strike intended for Jameson, intercepted by Marla. He sustained no major physical wound. He sustained the wound.

Cumulative physical sequelae: low-grade chronic tinnitus (the cigar-ear-tilt is in part a hearing-side accommodation in his good ear); probable mild left-sided sensorineural hearing loss; chronic low back pain (the deskbound life plus the falls); osteoarthritic changes in the right shoulder (the pointing arm, the door-slamming arm); a knee that he favors going up stairs in later panels.

Psychological impact: each incident is metabolized into the editorial voice within forty-eight hours; none is processed as personal trauma in the felt sense. The Marla event is the exception — it is not metabolizable and has not been metabolized. The pattern of his subsequent silences (the file notes his uncharacteristic refusal to give interviews on certain anniversaries) is the closest he comes to a grief reaction.

---

## 7. DERMATOLOGICAL, ENDOCRINE, AND THE TOUPEE

**Androgenetic alopecia**, Hamilton-Norwood class likely VI by middle age, advancing. The toupee — variably acknowledged in canon, sometimes a hairpiece, sometimes claimed as the genuine flat-top brush — is the only continuous prosthesis in the file. It is medically trivial and psychologically diagnostic: the subject who polemicizes against masks wears one on his head every day. He adjusts it under stress (a tell), removes it in moments of unguarded private affect with Marla (the only person in the record to have seen him without it without consequence), and treats its possible exposure as a near-catastrophic threat. The wig is the Spider-Man mask he is allowed to keep.

**Rosacea**, presumptive, mild to moderate, papulopustular and erythematotelangiectatic mixed. The nasal flush is permanent in later years.

**Diabetes mellitus, type 2**, probable from middle age, given the body habitus, diet, inactivity, family history (presumed), and chronic cortisol load. Likely metformin-managed; HbA1c probably borderline-to-poor; the cardiac risk multiplier this introduces is non-trivial and folds back into §5.

**Thyroid:** no documented pathology; the energy and the irritability are temperament and HPA, not hyperthyroid.

**Vision:** presbyopic from middle age; reading glasses on a chain or pushed up onto the toupee — observed; bifocals in later period. No documented retinal pathology, though chronic uncontrolled hypertension predicts low-grade hypertensive retinopathy on fundoscopy.

**Dentition:** intact, stained from cigar and coffee, probable periodontal disease given the same exposures and the irregular dental attendance of a man who treats appointments as enemy actions.

---

## 8. SUBSTANCES

**Tobacco.** Cigars, daily, multiple, across the entire canonical period until the post-MI reduction; brand reads as a mid-range American or Dominican, not the Cuban affectation of a poseur — this is a working cigar, used as gesture, weapon, and pacifier as much as combusted product. Cumulative pack-year-equivalent exposure is substantial. Pulmonary consequences: chronic productive cough (the throat-clear that opens his sentences), reduced exercise tolerance, near-certain mild-to-moderate COPD by late period, elevated risk for oral, laryngeal, and bladder cancer that has not, in the record, manifested. Post-MI he is told to stop; he reduces; he probably does not fully quit, substituting unlit cigars as oral fixation devices (the famous chewed-end cigar in later panels is consistent with this).

**Alcohol.** Notably moderate. He is not a tabloid-publisher drunk. A scotch at dinner, a beer at a Bugle softball game, a champagne flute at a wedding. The absence of alcohol abuse in a man with his trauma load and cardiovascular profile is one of the file's most distinguishing positive findings and is consistent with the §3 reading that his defenses are intellectualizing and somatic rather than chemical. He does not want to be less aware. He wants to be more right.

**Caffeine.** Extreme. Multiple cups of black coffee daily, beginning before dawn. Contributory to the hypertension, the ulcer, the arrhythmia risk, the sleep deficit, and the tremor that appears in his hands during the late-afternoon trough.

**Prescription compliance.** Episodic. Improves post-MI; degrades when work intensifies; relapses to baseline within months of any health scare unless Marla (and later, after her death, Robbie or a long-tenured assistant) is enforcing the pillbox.

**Recreational/illicit:** none in record. The man would rather die than be impaired in a meeting.

---

## 9. SURGICAL AND PROCEDURAL HISTORY

- Almost certain appendectomy or cholecystectomy at some point in middle age — the standard middle-aged-American-male abdominal surgical entry — though not explicit in canon.
- Cardiac catheterization with probable PCI/stenting, post-MI.
- Multiple ED presentations for chest pain, hypertensive urgency, syncope, blunt trauma from costumed incidents.
- Endoscopy/colonoscopy at age-appropriate intervals, presumed; the screening compliance is probably poor and probably enforced by Marla in life.
- Dental procedures, irregular.

No major reconstructive surgery; no orthopedic hardware; no transplant; no oncologic procedure on record.

---

## 10. TRANSFORMATIONS AND ENHANCEMENT EXPOSURE

Subject himself has not, in the canonical record, been subjected to a successful biological transformation. This is itself a notable medical fact in a person of his exposure profile.

- **Adjacency to mutagenic and symbiotic agents:** repeated, across decades — the Scorpion's mutagenesis, Venom's symbiote, Spider-Island's transformative outbreak (during which he was at elevated exposure risk as Mayor and was almost certainly medically screened and prophylactically treated).
- **Spider-Island specifically:** the citywide arachnid mutation arc places him at near-certain exposure; his non-transformation is either narratively elided or attributable to whatever intervention was deployed. The relevant medical detail is that he sat through the screening, the quarantine procedures, and the pharmaceutical or genetic countermeasures — and did not editorialize against them. He believes in public health when it is his own life on the line. This is a small datum and a large character disclosure.
- **Familial transformation exposure:** his son's repeated and severe biological alterations (Man-Wolf via the moongem; later cosmic transformations) make Jonah a chronic medical-anxiety carrier and a frequent occupant of hospital waiting rooms across decades. The cortisol load from this alone, in a man with his cardiac substrate, is medically material. He has sat at the bedside of an adult child who was variably human more times than any civilian father in the record. The toll is invisible in his editorials and visible in his face.

---

## 11. DISABILITIES

None formally adjudicated. Functionally: chronic low back pain, mild hearing loss, presbyopia, post-MI exercise limitation, episodic angina, the cumulative slowing of a man in his eighth decade with the cardiovascular history above. He refuses every accommodation that can be refused. The cane that briefly appears in late-period panels is discarded as soon as possible. The wheelchair after the MI was tolerated for the legally minimum distance to the curb.

---

## 12. INTEGRATED PSYCHOLOGICAL IMPACT — THE BODY AS THE FILE'S MOST RELIABLE WITNESS

The single most important interpretive principle for this medical history: **the somatic record is the truth-telling instrument the subject cannot edit.** The editorial voice can argue anything. The ulcer cannot. The MI cannot. The flush at the carotid cannot. The toupee adjustment in the moment of cognitive dissonance cannot. Every condition in this file is, in part, an act of the body refusing to ratify a fiction the mind requires.

The ulcer says: the rage is not righteousness, it is a wound in the gut.
The hypertension says: the certainty is not certainty, it is a vessel under pressure.
The MI says: the Scorpion was not justice, it was a debt, and here is the interest.
The toupee says: I, who hate masks, wear one.
The cigar says: I need something in my mouth that is not a feeling.
The sober record says: I will not be impaired, because the impairment I fear is my father's, and I will die before I become him.
The Marla-death silence says: there is one thing in this life I cannot turn into an editorial, and her name was Marla.

The medical history is, therefore, not adjacent to the psychological profile in §3 and the psychiatric formulation in §4 — it is their primary substantiation. The body has been writing the true dossier all along; this section merely transcribes it.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — J. JONAH JAMESON, JR.

*Cross-reference: Sections 2 (Medical) and 3 (Psychological). This atlas catalogs the body as instrument and as evidence. The subject's somatic register is unusually legible — he is not a man who has invested in concealment of affect, and the body has therefore become a high-resolution readout for those trained to look. Surveillance teams across three decades of file accumulation report extraordinary consistency: Jameson at 73 moves and breathes recognizably as Jameson at 38. The substrate does not change. The amplitude does.*

---

## 1. BUILD, FRAME, AND BASELINE STANCE

Five-foot-ten in his prime, possibly five-nine by the late-period file as cervical compression accumulates. Mesomorphic with a thickening waistline that he has carried since his forties — the Bugle-desk waist, accumulated from chair time and not from indulgence (see §4, eating). Neck thick, trapezii overdeveloped from a lifetime of shouting into telephones with the receiver pinched between shoulder and ear. Hands disproportionately broad for the frame, fingers blunt, knuckles enlarged — the hands of a man who jabs at things with them.

**Standing baseline.** Weight forward over the balls of the feet, never neutral. Feet set wider than hip-width, often at a slight outward angle — a stance optimized for confrontation rather than locomotion. Shoulders elevated approximately one centimeter above neutral at rest; he is always slightly *bracing*. Chin carried forward of the spine's plumb line by two to three centimeters — the classic "presenting" jaw of the chronically combative. Mild lumbar hyperlordosis with associated anterior pelvic tilt, the postural signature of someone who has stood at podiums and over desks more than he has sat in proper chairs.

**Seated baseline.** Does not sit so much as occupy. Lands hard. Leans back in the executive chair with one ankle crossed over the opposite knee — the open, territorial "figure-four" posture, never the closed European leg-cross. Both elbows on the chair arms unless one hand is engaged with cigar or phone, in which case the free elbow is on the desk. He does not slump; the spine remains engaged even when reclined, because the obliques are always faintly contracted. He cannot be observed at rest in any room he considers his own.

**Gait.** Heel-strike heavy; audible across a marble lobby. Arm swing on the right side broader than the left (right arm is his gesticulation arm and stays warmed up). Walks with the head leading, not the chest — neck-first, like a man entering a fight. Pace approximately 110–120 steps per minute, which is unusually fast for a man his age and weight; corridor surveillance consistently records subordinates breaking into a half-jog to keep up. Pivots sharply at doorways without slowing. Will not yield right-of-way in a hallway encounter unless the obstacle is female, elderly, or pushing a cart — three classes for which the courtesy is automatic and unhesitating.

---

## 2. THE HEAD AND FACE — TAXONOMY OF EXPRESSION

The face is the most surveilled real estate in the file. It does not modulate well; what passes through it is broadcast.

**Forehead and brow.** Deep horizontal frontalis furrows, three of them, etched permanently by sixty years of indignation. The corrugator complex is overdeveloped; the vertical "elevens" between the brows are visible at rest. Brow asymmetry: left brow lifts independently when skeptical (the "and you expect me to believe" microexpression, deployed reflexively in conversation with anyone under forty). Both brows compress and lower when angry; both lift in the rare register of genuine surprise, which the face is poorly practiced in.

**Eyes.** Small relative to the face, set deep under heavy supraorbital ridges. Color shifts in the record across artists but the canonical read is pale, gray-blue, with reduced affect-lubrication — they do not water easily. Tear film inadequate; he blinks at roughly half the population average rate when concentrated (six to eight blinks per minute against a norm of fifteen to twenty), which produces the famous "stare" and accounts for the chronic conjunctival irritation noted in §2 of the medical record. When agitated the blink rate triples abruptly, then collapses again. Pupillary response normal but pupils tend toward constriction under fluorescent office light — he reads paper documents at unusually close range, suggesting uncorrected presbyopia he refuses to acknowledge with bifocals; uses cheaters pulled from a drawer when no one is watching.

**The mustache.** Toothbrush/Hitlerian rectangle, kept at approximately one centimeter in height, never wider than the philtrum. Trimmed by him personally with manicure scissors, weekly, at the bathroom mirror — a ritual performed in his shorts and an unbuttoned dress shirt at approximately 6:15 a.m. The mustache is a face-organizer; it gives the mouth a frame and makes the lip's movements legible. He touches it unconsciously with the pad of the right index finger when thinking — smooths it left-to-right, then once right-to-left. Three smooths means an idea is forming. Five or more means he is stalling for time.

**The hair.** The flat-top brush is canonical and contested: in some periods plausibly his own (gray-white, stiffened with pomade or wax), in others openly a hairpiece. Surveillance treats it as a hairpiece in maturity. He never touches it in public. He adjusts it in mirrors only when alone — washroom mirrors, the back of a spoon, the dark glass of an office window when he thinks the reflection is too dim to be seen by others. The hairpiece is the single most defended object on his person and the only reliable indicator of vanity in a man who otherwise displays none.

**Mouth.** Thin upper lip, slightly fuller lower. Resting position is a faint downturn at the corners — not a frown, but a default that reads as displeased to anyone meeting him for the first time. When speaking publicly, the mouth opens wider than the words require; he over-articulates, possibly compensating for the cigar-and-shouting roughness of the voice. When listening, the mouth often holds slightly open with the lower lip relaxed — a "ready to interrupt" position that is itself a form of pressure on the speaker.

**Jaw.** Masseter hypertrophy visible bilaterally; he clenches. Bruxism almost certainly present nocturnally (Marla's prior testimony in the *Spectacular* run references his "grinding"). The jaw is the primary tension-storage site. When stress passes a threshold the jaw locks and the cheeks flatten; this is the warning sign that an eruption is within ninety seconds.

**Coloration as gauge.** The most reliable real-time stress meter in the file. Baseline complexion is florid-ruddy, slightly weathered. Mild irritation: pink flush across the malar prominences. Moderate anger: red migrates upward to the forehead and downward into the neck above the collar. Severe rage: the red becomes uniform from clavicle to scalp line, the temporal veins distend visibly, and the periorbital area paradoxically *whitens* against the surrounding flush — a vasomotor sign closely associated, in his clinical history, with imminent hypertensive episode. Surveillance protocol: when the temples vein and the eye-rings whiten, evacuate non-essential personnel and ready cardiac response.

---

## 3. HANDS, GESTURE, AND THE CIGAR ECONOMY

The hands are the second readout. He talks with them constantly.

**Resting hand position.** Right hand on or near the cigar (active or inactive). Left hand either flat on the desk, fingers spread, or curled around a coffee cup. He does not steeple, does not bridge, does not engage in any of the deliberative-executive hand displays. His hands are working tools, not display ornaments.

**Primary gestures, in order of frequency:**
- **The jab.** Right index finger extended, other fingers curled, driven forward at the listener from elbow level. Used to emphasize a point or to apportion blame; can be sustained for entire sentences, the finger pumping with each stressed syllable. Distance from listener's chest at full extension: typically 30–45 centimeters; he is a close-talker when angry.
- **The slam.** Open right palm brought down flat on the desk, usually following a declarative statement. Always the right hand. Always the desk; he does not slam on tabletops he does not own. Force is calibrated — it is performative, not destructive; the desk has never been damaged.
- **The dismissive wave.** Right hand at shoulder level, palm down, swept laterally outward. Used to terminate a conversation or to discard an idea. Often paired with a half-turn of the head away from the speaker.
- **The "get out."** Right hand extended toward the door, palm vertical, index finger sometimes pointing. The phrase need not be spoken; the gesture suffices and is universally understood by Bugle staff.
- **The cigar-jab.** The unlit cigar held between thumb and first two fingers, used as an extension of the index finger for pointing. The jab made with a cigar is harder to ignore than the jab made with bare flesh; he knows this.
- **The lapel-grab.** Reserved for moments of physical confrontation, rare but on record. He has grabbed lapels of: Norman Osborn (pre-revelation), at least two senators, a Spider-Slayer pilot, and Robbie Robertson once (instantly regretted, the only such instance, never repeated).

**The cigar — full operational profile.** Mid-grade Dominican or Honduran corona, never premium Cuban (he is reflexively suspicious of luxury affect, and Cuban contraband would compromise the publisher's ethics he polemicizes about). Kept in a humidor on the credenza behind the desk, not the desk itself — he must turn to retrieve one, which gives a conversational pause its physical correlate. Cuts with a guillotine cutter; lights with wooden matches, not a lighter, struck on the matchbook itself with one hand. The lighting ritual takes approximately eleven seconds and is the longest period of uninterrupted silence he reliably produces in a working day. Smoking pattern: he does not inhale — pure mouth-and-jowl draw, exhaled upward and to his right, away from his interlocutor (a courtesy he is not consciously aware of extending). Burns through approximately one-third of a cigar before letting it die; relights twice, then discards. Daily consumption at peak: four to six cigars. Post-cardiac event: reduced to one or two, then to chewing unlit cigars, then in late-period files to chewing on a wooden swizzle stick or a pen cap as substitute. The oral need does not extinguish; only the smoke does.

**Cigar as weapon.** Used to control conversational space (smoke as territory), to punctuate (jab, point), and to delay (the lighting ritual buys him time when he does not yet know what he thinks). Loss of the cigar mid-confrontation — knocked from his hand, stolen by a child, extinguished by spilled coffee — is one of the few events that produces visible disorientation; he loses the rhythm and must reset.

**Fine motor.** Surprisingly delicate when writing. He drafts editorials in longhand first, in a small, dense, slightly leftward-leaning cursive on legal pads, before dictating or typing. The cigar is set aside during writing; the writing hand is separated, ritualistically, from the gesturing hand.

---

## 4. ORAL, VOCAL, AND RESPIRATORY

**Voice baseline.** Baritone, gravelled by decades of cigars and shouting, with a pronounced outer-borough New York substrate (Queens-inflected, not Brooklyn; the vowels are flatter and the cadence faster). Speaks at a baseline volume approximately 15 dB above conversational norm — he is loud in rooms where loudness is not required, and this is not a choice. Range: he can drop to a gravel-whisper during confidential conversation (rare, used with Robbie and Marla almost exclusively) and can amplify to a parade-ground bellow without strain; the bellow is the home register.

**Speech patterns.** Rapid, declarative, comma-poor. Average word count per sentence approximately fourteen. Frequent use of rhetorical questions answered immediately by himself. Profanity register: aggressive but old-fashioned — "blasted," "confounded," "for cripes' sake," "what in the name of" — a generationally specific avoidance of the genuinely obscene that traces, plausibly, to his mother's standards rather than his own. Modern recordings show some drift toward harsher language but he remains, by tabloid-publisher norms, a clean speaker.

**Vocal tics.**
- The throat-clear before a difficult statement — two short, dry clears, then the statement.
- The "Hah!" — a single explosive monosyllable used to dismiss a claim he considers absurd; not a laugh. The genuine laugh is different (see below).
- The "Now you listen to me" preamble, used approximately fifteen to twenty times per working day, often when no listening is actually required.
- The trailing "...understand?" — terminal question tag attached to instructions, demanding affirmative response. Surveillance recordings show staff have learned to answer with "Yes, Mr. Jameson" within 0.4 seconds of the tag; longer pauses produce repetition at higher volume.

**Laugh.** Rare and notable. A genuine Jameson laugh is a short bark — "HA" — followed by two or three lower "huh-huh-huh" exhalations and then a brief silence as he composes himself. Triggers: physical comedy involving the pompous (a senator slipping on ice), Robbie's deadpan, his grandson's mispronunciations, certain newsroom catastrophes once they have safely concluded. He does not laugh at jokes told to him; he laughs at situations he observes.

**Breathing.** Diaphragmatic capacity reduced by decades of seated work and abdominal weight. Mouth-breather under stress; nose-breather at rest. Audible exhalations through the nose ("snorts") are his most frequent affective punctuation — used to express skepticism, contempt, mild amusement, and impatience, distinguished from each other by duration and accompanying brow position. Trained observers can taxonomize at least six distinct snorts in his repertoire.

---

## 5. GROOMING AND PERSONAL MAINTENANCE

**Shaving.** Daily, by safety razor, before 6 a.m. Never electric — he considers electric shaves a kind of moral shortcut. Splash of inexpensive aftershave (Aqua Velva or Old Spice; the record varies, but the price point is consistent). Small recurring nick at the right jaw line, evidence of speed over care.

**Dress.** The suit is uniform, not fashion. Three-piece in earlier decades, two-piece since the late 1990s. Charcoal, navy, or rarely brown. White or pale-blue shirt, never patterned. Tie always knotted in a full Windsor — the wide, symmetrical knot that fills the collar entirely. Tie loosened by approximately one centimeter from the collar by 11 a.m.; loosened a further centimeter by 3 p.m.; loosened to roughly the second shirt button by 7 p.m. and removed entirely if he stays past 9. The progression is a clock. Shoes: black or cordovan oxfords, leather soles, kept polished by him personally on Sunday evenings in a basement workshop ritual that predates Marla and was preserved after her death. Cufflinks: simple, often given by Marla; he turns the left one with his right thumb when nervous.

**The toupee maintenance.** Conducted in absolute privacy. The piece is brushed with a dedicated boar-bristle brush, cleaned weekly with a specialized shampoo, and stored on a faceless wooden form in his bedroom closet at night. Replacement pieces are ordered through a single supplier (cash, by mail, under a name that is not his) at approximately three-year intervals. He has never been photographed without the piece in any context he consented to.

**Smell signature.** Cigar smoke (Type 1 dominant), aftershave (Type 2), the printer's-ink-and-newsprint smell that the Bugle building deposits in his clothing (Type 3 ambient), faint coffee on the breath, occasional antacid chalk. The composite is recognizable in an elevator before he enters it.

---

## 6. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Schedule.** Wakes at 5:30 a.m. without alarm, has done so since his Korean War-era Army service. Asleep by 11:30 p.m. on workdays, midnight on weekends. Net sleep: six hours, chronically insufficient by clinical standards but stable.

**Sleep quality.** Poor. Onset latency twenty-plus minutes despite exhaustion — the editorial mind does not switch off. Nocturnal awakenings two to four times per night, often to urinate (BPH, age-appropriate, untreated by his choice). REM compression likely; he reports few dreams and the ones he reports are anxiety-flavored (the press deadline missed, the front page blank, his father's voice from another room).

**Sleep posture.** Supine, head elevated on two pillows — antireflux positioning forced by the ulcer history. Snores heavily, mouth open, with periodic apneic pauses (untreated OSA strongly suspected and consistent with the cardiovascular profile). Bruxism throughout the night, audible.

**Nightmares.** Specific recurring contents inferable from canon: his father's house; the moment of authorizing the Stillwell procedure; Marla's death in the Spider-Slayer; the unmasking conversation with Peter. These cluster around anniversaries and around current stressors that pattern-match to them. He does not discuss them.

---

## 7. EATING, DRINKING, AND ORAL CONSUMPTION

**Breakfast.** Black coffee, two cups, plus a bagel with butter or a single piece of dry rye toast — eaten at the desk, with the morning papers (four to six broadsheets and tabloids, his own last). Skipped entirely under deadline.

**Lunch.** Almost always at the desk. Pastrami on rye, mustard, no pickle (the pickle aggravates the ulcer and he resents this fact). Coffee, third cup. Occasionally a hot dog from a specific cart on Sixth Avenue whose vendor he has known for thirty years and tips disproportionately. He does not do business lunches; he considers them a waste of working hours and an opportunity for being managed.

**Dinner.** Eaten at home when Marla was alive, in the kitchen, with the television off. Post-Marla, dinner has degraded — takeout containers at the desk, the kitchen rarely used. He has been observed by household surveillance eating cold leftover Chinese food standing at the refrigerator on at least one documented occasion.

**Snacking.** Hard candies and chalky antacid tablets are interchangeable in his right pocket; he sometimes confuses them and notices only after the second chew. Sucks on hard candy when the cigar is unavailable. Caffeine intake throughout the day: six to eight cups of coffee at the Bugle (drip, milk no sugar, in a specific mug — the white one with the chipped rim; the chip points away from him when he drinks). He notices when the mug is replaced.

**Alcohol.** Genuinely moderate. A single scotch at home in the evening on weekdays, two on Saturdays, none on Sundays. He does not drink in his office. He does not drink at lunch. He has been observed visibly impaired exactly twice in the surveillance record — both following Marla's death.

**Eating posture.** Eats fast, head down, elbows wide. Napkin tucked into the collar at home (Marla disapproved; he persisted); never in public. Chews loudly. Wipes mouth with the back of the hand if no napkin is to hand.

---

## 8. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE PATTERN

The file is appropriately sparse here, drawn from inference and from Marla's incidental on-page testimony.

**Orientation and history.** Heterosexual, monogamous within marriages. Two marriages on record: first wife Joan (deceased, killed by mugging — a foundational trauma in his anti-crime journalistic stance and not unrelated to his anti-vigilante stance, since the muggers were never caught and no costumed hero arrived to help); second to Marla Madison (also deceased). Between marriages he was conspicuously solitary; no record of dating, no record of casual encounters. He is not a man with appetite for novelty.

**Intimacy with Marla.** Affectionate in private. Touch register: his right hand on the small of her back when entering a room together; her hand on his forearm to defuse him when his volume rose. He kissed her on the temple, not the mouth, in greeting and parting — a tenderness habit that surveillance records as utterly consistent across their entire marriage. In the bedroom (inferable from incidental panels and Marla's dialogue), he reportedly slept with one arm draped across her waist. He talked to her after lights-out; this was the only time of day his voice descended to its true register, below the public bark.

**Post-Marla.** The body language of bereavement persists: he still angles his right hand for the small-of-back gesture on entering rooms and catches himself; he still leaves the left half of his bed undisturbed. No subsequent romantic interest on record. The chapter is closed.

**Physical affection generally.** Outside marriage, severely restricted. Shakes hands firmly, two pumps, releases. Will clasp a male shoulder in moments of high feeling (Robbie, John, Peter post-unmasking once). Does not hug except to his son, and to his son only on the rare occasions when John has been restored to human form after a transformation — these are documented, full, two-armed embraces, held longer than the photographed moment permits, and they constitute the most uninhibited physical affection in the entire record.

---

## 9. STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFTS — THE SOMATIC SWITCHBOARD

**Calm (rare, observable mostly in the early morning at home before papers arrive, or on Sundays in the shoe-polishing ritual).** Shoulders drop to true neutral. Jaw unclenches; a small underbite becomes visible. Voice modulates downward by roughly a third in volume. Hands settle. Breathing deepens, becomes audible at rest. Face loses approximately five years.

**Working baseline (most observed state).** Described in §1–§4 above. Productive irritability. The mode in which most of the file material is recorded.

**Mild stress (deadline pressure, staff incompetence, ordinary obstruction).** Volume up. Cigar lit and re-lit more frequently. Pacing emerges — three steps left, three right, behind the desk, hands behind back. Jab gesture deployed more readily. Pink flush across malars. Antacid tablet count rises.

**Moderate stress (financial pressure on the paper, Spider-Man on the front page of a competitor, his son in distress).** Pacing becomes continuous. Cigar burns hot and is drawn on more aggressively. Voice cracks under sustained shouting. Forehead beads with sweat at the hairline. Flush extends to neck. Speech becomes more declarative and less listening-permeable. He stops answering the phone. Left hand goes to lower sternum unconsciously — palpating the ulcer site or the cardiac region; the gesture is identical and he cannot distinguish them.

**High stress (genuine cris


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## 6.1 The Origin Substrate

To read Jameson's adult relational behavior, one begins where the etiology begins: in the apartment of David Jonah Jameson Sr. — decorated soldier in the public record, batterer in the private one, and in the modernized backstory (Waid, *Family Business*, 2014; reinforced in subsequent Slott material) a bigamist and confidence man whose second family was kept under a separate name for years. The developmental input here is unusually clean to diagnose because it has three distinct corruptions stacked on one another:

1. **The man with the most power in the room used it to hurt people the child loved.**
2. **The man with the most power in the room presented a public face entirely at odds with the private one — and was praised for the public face.**
3. **The child's mother, whatever her constraints, did not extract him from this environment.**

The attachment-theoretic prediction from this loading is specific. One does not get a securely attached adult. One does not, however, necessarily get the disorganized profile of more extreme abuse cases, because the abuse — by Jameson's own oblique accounts — was patterned, predictable, and centered on the father. Predictability, even of harm, produces *organized* insecure attachment rather than disorganization.

What the canon shows the adult to be is **insecure-preoccupied with strong avoidant overlay** — a profile sometimes called "fearful-avoidant" in attachment literature, though Jameson's variant tilts preoccupied because he cannot in fact tolerate solitude or distance and uses his subordinates and institutions as continuous proximity objects. He needs people near him constantly; he cannot let them matter overtly; the contradiction is the engine.

## 6.2 The Bonding Sequence — A Reproducible Four-Stage Protocol

Across sixty years of published material the subject runs almost every significant relationship through the same four-stage sequence. The stages are observable in his bond with Peter Parker, Robbie Robertson, Betty Brant, Ben Urich, Glory Grant, Marla Madison, Norah Winters, and — in inverted, foreshortened form — with his son John. The protocol is not chosen; it is the only one he has.

**Stage One: Dominance display.** First contact is hostile, loud, territorial. He insults the candidate's competence, appearance, ambition, or all three within the first ninety seconds. He establishes — vocally, with the cigar as pointer — that he is the senior animal in the room and that the relationship will operate on his terms. The display is performative and, importantly, *standardized*: he runs the same opening on a Pulitzer-level investigative reporter and on a stringer delivering film. This is not assessment. This is throat-clearing. What he is actually doing is generating enough noise to mask the fact that he is reading the other person closely — for posture, for flinch, for whether they will lie to him.

**Stage Two: Loyalty test, usually unconscious on his part.** Within the first six months he will manufacture (or, more often, simply fail to suppress) a situation that costs the new person something — an unpaid expense, a public dressing-down in front of staff, an assignment designed to fail, a withheld credit, a deliberately impossible deadline. The test is not whether the person succeeds. The test is whether the person *stays*, and whether, when they speak back to him, they speak with their own voice rather than a performance of contrition. Sycophants are filtered out here. Cowards are filtered out here. He despises both because he sees both in himself.

**Stage Three: Grudging trust, signalled by operational delegation.** The person who survives Stages One and Two begins to receive, without ceremony, the things Jameson actually values: access to the morning conference, the right to argue with him in front of others, the assumption that their copy will run, the small budgetary discretions he denies everyone else. He will continue to bark at them — louder, sometimes, than at strangers — but the content of the barking becomes formulaic where it was once targeted. This is his version of affection. Long-term Bugle staff learn to read the difference between the bark-as-territory-marking (safe, almost warm) and the bark-as-actual-threat (rare, dangerous, follow-through likely).

**Stage Four: Permanent unspoken bond.** Once a person is in, they are in for life, and Jameson will absorb extraordinary costs to keep them there. He posts bail. He keeps the health insurance on staff during cash crises. He attends funerals — Marla's father's, Ben Urich's wife's, Robbie's family events — and stands at the back, having forgotten to take the cigar out of his mouth, and leaves without speaking to anyone. He never names the bond. The closest he ever comes to declaring it is firing the person (always over something disproportionate), then rehiring them within forty-eight hours with a raise he refuses to discuss. The firing-and-rehiring cycle, recurrent across Peter Parker's tenure and documented with Betty Brant and others, is a relational tic with diagnostic value: he literally cannot maintain a stable expressed affection, so he discharges the intolerable affect by ejecting the love object and then reabsorbs them when the discharge has cleared.

## 6.3 The Specific Templates

**Robertson, Joseph "Robbie."** The closest thing in the file to a fully functional adult attachment outside the marriage. Robbie is the man who can say "Jonah" — first name — in a tone that ends an editorial argument. He is the only employee who has ever publicly contradicted Jameson without consequence, and the only one whose silence Jameson registers as more meaningful than his speech. The frame-up arc (Tombstone, late 1980s into the 1990s) is the empirical proof of the bond: Jameson, against every commercial and political instinct, kept Robbie on the masthead, paid his legal fees through his own accounts, and visited the prison without telling staff. He never spoke of any of it. Robbie functions in the relational system as the *good father* counterweight to David Sr. — the older Black man (in Jameson's experience, racially coded outside his original tribal frame, which matters in his early-1970s acquisition of the friendship) who is morally serious, calm, and does not lie. Jameson trusts him with the institution. He has never trusted anyone else with the institution.

**Brant, Betty.** The relationship is paternal-fraternal, complicated by her early grief (brother killed adjacent to Spider-Man activity) which Jameson absorbed without naming. He kept her employed through years of her own instability and through her marriage to Ned Leeds and its aftermath. The template here shows another tic: he protects women in his orbit through *employment continuity* rather than expressed concern. The job is the affection.

**Urich, Ben.** Rivalrous-fraternal. Urich is the journalist Jameson wishes he had remained when he chose to become a publisher. The relationship runs on mutual irritation that masks deep professional respect. Jameson lets Urich pursue stories he would suppress in anyone else, including stories that embarrass the Bugle, because Urich represents the road not taken and Jameson is, in his way, paying tithe to it.

**Grant, Glory.** Personal assistant for the bulk of the published period. The relationship is a study in his inability to express dependency: he needs her completely, runs the office through her, would not survive a week without her — and addresses her in a register one octave below the one he uses for everyone else, which is the closest thing to tenderness his voice produces in a professional setting.

**Madison, Marla.** The exception that proves the structural rule. With Marla, Stages One and Two collapse almost entirely; he met her as a scientist (Spider-Slayer consulting, ironically) and the dominance display did not take because she was content-secure and unflinching, which short-circuited the test. The marriage, across decades of canon, is the only relationship in which Jameson is regularly observed *quiet*. He listens to her. He removes the cigar in her presence. He brings her tea. He does not raise his voice in their apartment, with one or two writer-marked exceptions where the writer was making a point about external stress bleeding into the home. Her death (Spider-Island, by a Spider-Slayer descendant) is the second somatic-emotional collapse in the file (§2) precisely because she was the only relationship in which his defenses were genuinely lowered, and her loss removed his only experience of being known without being attacked or attacking back. He has not, in the canonical record, replaced this. He cannot. The architecture isn't there to build it twice.

**Jameson, John III ("Jack").** Father-son. The relational template inverts here in interesting ways: he displays Stage One dominance with his adult son even into late canon, but the displays land softer because the underlying terror — that John will be hurt, will be transformed, will not come back from orbit — is so loud in Jonah that it leaks through the bark. With John's recurrent transformations (Man-Wolf, Stargod, possessions) Jameson exhibits the only affect in the entire record that is *unmodulated*: open paternal fear, occasional tears, willingness to plead. He has begged Spider-Man's help for John on multiple occasions and remembered nothing of the editorial line the next morning. The relationship is also where his deepest avoidance lives: he loves John fiercely and cannot tell him so, and has constructed a lifetime of overprotective opposition (discouraging the astronaut career, criticizing John's choices in women, undermining his independence) as the only vocabulary he has for the love. John, to his credit, has learned to translate.

**Parker, Peter.** The most analytically rich relationship in the file because it occupies two registers simultaneously for thirty in-universe years. *Surface register*: difficult employee, perpetual irritant, the kid he can pay below scale and yell at. *Deeper register, visible in the unguarded moments scattered through the Stern, DeMatteis, Slott, and Spencer runs*: surrogate son. The evidence is granular. He never actually fires Peter for the things Peter does that would have fired any other freelancer. He covers for Peter with Aunt May. He attended the wedding. He gave career-changing assignments in moments where, on the editorial record, he should have been freezing Peter out. He kept the kid in his orbit for decades. After the unmasking — when Peter tells him directly that he is Spider-Man — the protocol shorts out: the surrogate son turns out to be the symbolic father (Spider-Man as the powerful masked man, by his etiology David Sr.'s descendant), and Jameson cannot hold both readings at once without his entire defense structure cracking. His behavior in the post-unmasking arcs (initial rage, slow reorientation, podcast advocacy that overshoots into hagiography) is exactly what attachment theory predicts when a person discovers that two contradictory internal working models were actually one person all along. He overcorrects because the only stable position is to merge the two readings into something usable, and "Spider-Man supporter" lets him keep Peter without confronting in full what the prior thirty years cost.

## 6.4 Distrust — The Pattern of Suspicion

Jameson's distrust is *targeted* rather than diffuse — a fact that disqualifies the Paranoid Personality differential (§4) but also illuminates the relational template. He distrusts, in declining order of intensity: **masked or anonymous power; men in positions of public trust whose private behavior is hidden; people who flatter him; people who don't push back; people who try to leave.**

The first three categories all map onto the father. The fourth maps onto the mother (insufficient pushback equals insufficient protection equals complicity). The fifth maps onto every developmental experience of abandonment he has metabolized into a relational rule: if you signal an intent to depart, he will preemptively eject you, because being the leaver is tolerable and being left is not.

He extends operational trust very wide within his in-group (Robbie can be told anything; Marla was told everything) and almost zero trust outside it. New entrants must serve the four-stage probation. People who fail the probation are not just disliked; they are *categorized* — and Jameson's categories, once assigned, are exceptionally expensive to revise. ASM #169-170, the "Spider-Man Guilty?" retraction, is the rare documented case of category revision under evidentiary pressure, and it took a stacked, public, undeniable evidence load to produce it.

## 6.5 Betrayal — How He Reads It, How He Performs It

He reads betrayal *primarily as concealment* rather than as harm. A subordinate who steals from him and admits it can be reabsorbed; a subordinate who lies about a minor matter is exiled. This is the father-template at full strength: the harm itself is metabolizable; the *hiddenness* of the harm is what shatters the working model. Peter Parker's three decades of concealment hit him harder than any superhero punch ever did because the structure of the deception precisely replicated David Sr.'s second family — a parallel hidden life maintained alongside the visible one.

He performs betrayal, when he performs it, in a specific signature: he uses *institutional voice* rather than personal voice. He will write the editorial that destroys you rather than calling you a liar in private. He will file the lawsuit (against Peter Parker, post-unmasking, for fraudulent photo fees) rather than the angry letter. The institution is the cudgel because the institution is the part of him that feels safe to wield; personal confrontation requires the body, and the body, by his own admission, is where he is not brave.

## 6.6 Repair — The Wordless Protocol

Jameson does not apologize in proportion. This is the most consistent finding in the relational record and the one that has cost him the most. The post-unmasking arc is the clearest case: he never says, to Peter Parker, a sentence adequate to thirty years of public defamation and material harm. He cannot. The apology-act requires the very thing his defense structure was built to prevent — sustained, undefended occupation of the position of having been wrong about something central.

What he does instead is a **behavioral apology, executed through provision and proximity.** He shows up. He sends work. He pays bills he wasn't asked to pay. He defends the wronged party in public against third parties. He changes his editorial line, sometimes overcorrecting (the podcast hagiography). With Robbie, after periods of conflict, he assigns plum stories. With Marla, after fights, he came home with the wrong flowers, having forgotten which ones she liked, but he came home with flowers, and she — being the only person who fully read the system — understood the gesture for what it was.

The repair is real. It is just chronically under-articulated, and the people closest to him have all had to learn his dialect. The ones who learned it kept him. The ones who didn't — and there are not many; the four-stage probation filters them — left and became part of the file of people he will not speak about.

## 6.7 Intimacy and Dependency — The Negative Space

Intimacy, in Jameson's life, occurs almost exclusively in *negative space*: in things not said, in cigars not lit when Marla had a headache, in doors closed quietly when John was sleeping after a transformation, in the long silence after Robbie said something Jonah didn't want to hear and Jonah, for once, did not interrupt. He cannot do declared intimacy. The declaration itself triggers the defense.

Dependency he experiences as humiliation and therefore disguises as command. He depends utterly on Glory Grant and addresses her as if she works for him (which she does, but the relationship's actual weight is the reverse). He depended utterly on Marla and never, in the record, said *I need you*; he said variants of *don't be ridiculous* when she said it to him, and meant the opposite. He depends on Robbie's moral compass and presents the dependence as tolerating Robbie's interference. He depended, for thirty years, on Peter Parker's photographs and on the structural presence of Spider-Man in his life as the organizing antagonist of his identity — and the unmasking exposed both dependencies at once, which is why the somatic and psychological cost of that revelation was so high.

## 6.8 The Master Template, Stated

Every Jonah Jameson relationship runs the same underlying program: **approach loudly to mask the reading; test for staying-power; once the person stays, install them as a permanent fixture and protect them through provision while continuing to bark at them as a means of keeping the affection deniable; never name the bond; never apologize in proportion; ride out the inevitable conflicts via the firing-and-rehiring cycle or its equivalents; in the rare moments of unguarded contact, remove the cigar, lower the voice, and briefly be the man the editorials describe.**

The template is a child's solution to an impossible house, perpetuated into a sixty-year adult life because it worked well enough — well enough to build a newspaper, raise a son, hold a marriage, run a city, and keep, for decades, the loyalty of people who had every operational reason to leave. It is also the reason he is, by his own diagnosis, a coward in the one register that matters most to him: the register of *saying the thing out loud, while the body is in the room*. He has built an entire life — masthead, mayoralty, microphone — to avoid having to do that. The people who love him have all learned to hear what he means in the spaces between what he says. The people who don't, never get past Stage Two.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7
## DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

*Subject: J. Jonah Jameson, Jr. Cross-reference §3 (Psychological), §4 (Psychiatric), §2 (Somatic). The architecture below is derived from sixty years of behavioral record and arranged from most primitive to most mature, with the operational footprint of each mechanism mapped to observable conduct.*

---

### 7.0 Architectural Overview

Jameson's defensive system is unusual in one respect that must be stated up front: it spans nearly the entire Vaillant hierarchy. He runs primitive defenses (splitting, projection, somatization) and mature defenses (sublimation, altruism via institution, humor — yes, humor, gallows-grade) in the same hour, sometimes the same sentence. This is not a fragmented system; it is an over-built one. The trauma load required a defensive apparatus capable of holding catastrophic affect, and what got built was a layered fortress that uses primitive walls at the perimeter and mature engineering at the keep. The outer ring is what most people see and most editors caricature. The inner ring is where the journalism gets made and the loyalties are kept.

The defenses fire in a reliable sequence under stress, and the sequence itself is diagnostic. Track it forward: somatization warns him before he is conscious of affect; reaction formation reframes the affect as moral conviction; projection assigns the affect's origin to an external target; displacement routes the discharge through that target; intellectualization (the editorial voice) converts the discharge into argument; sublimation, if the system has time and the target is appropriate, channels the residue into legitimate civic work. If the sequence is interrupted at any stage — typically by an unmissable piece of evidence, by family threat, or by Marla — the system collapses inward and the man briefly appears. He cannot tolerate that appearance for long, and the cycle restarts.

---

### 7.1 PRIMITIVE DEFENSES (Level I — Psychotic/Near-Psychotic Register)

These are rare in Jameson and largely absent from baseline functioning. They surface only under acute decompensation (MI antecedents, Marla's death, the Scorpion-as-Venom confrontation, the unmasking aftermath).

**7.1.1 Splitting.** Operates exclusively along the masked/unmasked axis. Masked = concealed = fraudulent = dangerous (the father-template, see §4 etiology). Unmasked, named, on-the-record = legitimate, arguable, civically valid. This split is so structural that it survives evidence: even after the unmasking, when Peter Parker is named and known to him, Jameson's first cognitive move is not to integrate Peter and Spider-Man but to oscillate between them — Peter is the photographer-son-figure he provided for; Spider-Man is the masked menace he editorialized against. Integration takes years of in-universe time and is never fully completed. Under acute stress the split reasserts: he can speak warmly of Peter and contemptuously of Spider-Man in adjacent sentences without registering the contradiction.

**7.1.2 Denial.** Selective and time-limited. He does not deny external facts well (he is too good a journalist); he denies internal facts powerfully. The denied content is consistent across decades: *I am afraid. I am responsible. I am the man my father made.* The denial is breached in three documented contexts only — the Sin-Eater confession, the post-Scorpion-confrontation hospitalization, and the immediate aftermath of Marla's death — and is rebuilt each time within weeks.

**7.1.3 Distortion (mild).** Restricted to the Spider-Man dossier. He misremembers details that complicate his thesis, foregrounds details that confirm it. This is not delusion (see §4 differential) — it is motivated reasoning operating at the perceptual layer. It is also, notably, the same cognitive distortion every committed editorialist runs; in Jameson it is just more visible because the target is wrong.

---

### 7.2 IMMATURE DEFENSES (Level II — Borderline Register)

These are his working stock. Most observed Jameson behavior is generated from this band.
